# <a name="removed-or-deprecated-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="75868-103">Fjernede eller forældede funktioner</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-103">Removed or deprecated features</span></span>

[!include [banner](../includes/banner.md)]

<span data-ttu-id="75868-104">I dette emne beskrives funktioner, der er blevet fjernet eller frarådes for Dynamics 365 for Finance and Operations.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-104">This topic describes features that have been removed or deprecated for Dynamics 365 for Finance and Operations.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="75868-105">En *fjernet* funktion er ikke længere tilgængelige i produktet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-105">A *removed* feature is no longer available in the product.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="75868-106">En *forældet* funktion er ikke i aktiv udvikling og fjernes muligvis i en senere opdatering.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-106">A *deprecated* feature is not in active development and may be removed in a future update.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="75868-107">Denne liste er beregnet til at hjælpe dig med at overveje disse fjernelser og forældelser for din egen planlægning.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-107">This list is intended to help you consider these removals and deprecations for your own planning.</span></span> 

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="75868-108">Fra og med Dynamics 365 for Finance and Operations-versionen fra juli 2017 med Platform update 8 er installationstyperne angivet for hver fjernet eller forældet funktion.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-108">Starting with the Dynamics 365 for Finance and Operations July 2017 release with platform update 8, the type of deployments are noted for each removed or deprecated feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-109">Alle de tidligere versioner, der er nævnt i dette emne, understøtter kun installationer i skyen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-109">All of the previous releases mentioned in this topic supported cloud deployments only.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="75868-110">Du kan finde detaljerede oplysninger om objekter i Finance and Operations i [Technical Reference-rapporterne](https://mbs.microsoft.com/customersource/northamerica/AX/downloads/reports/axtechrefrep).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-110">Detailed information about objects in Finance and Operations can be found in the [Technical reference reports](https://mbs.microsoft.com/customersource/northamerica/AX/downloads/reports/axtechrefrep).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-111">Du kan sammenligne de forskellige versioner af disse rapporter for at få mere at vide om objekter, der er ændret eller fjernet i hver version af Finance and Operations.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-111">You can compare the different versions of these reports to learn about objects that have changed or been removed in each version of Finance and Operations.</span></span>

## <a name="dynamics-365-for-finance-and-operations-1005-with-platform-update-29"></a><span data-ttu-id="75868-112">Dynamics 365 for Finance and Operations 10.0.5 med platformsopdatering 29</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-112">Dynamics 365 for Finance and Operations 10.0.5 with Platform update 29</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="75868-113">Dynamics 365 for Finance and Operations 10.0.5 med platformsopdatering 29 er tilgængelig for brugere i målgruppen som en del af en eksempelversion.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-113">Dynamics 365 for Finance and Operations 10.0.5 with Platform update 29 is available to targeted users as part of a preview release.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-114">Indholdet og funktionaliteten kan blive ændret.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-114">The content and the functionality are subject to change.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-115">Du kan finde flere oplysninger om frigivelser af eksempelversioner her: [Tilgængelighed af tjenesteopdatering](../../fin-and-ops/get-started/public-preview-releases.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-115">For more information about preview releases, see [Service update availability](../../fin-and-ops/get-started/public-preview-releases.md).</span></span>

### <a name="legacy-default-action-behavior"></a><span data-ttu-id="75868-167">Ældre standardhandlingers opførelse</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-167">Legacy default action behavior</span></span>

|------------|--------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="75868-168">**Årsagen til forældelsen/fjernelsen**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-168">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="75868-169">Den ældre opførelse for standardhandlinger i gitre resulterer i, at en uventet kolonne indeholder linket til standardhandlingen, efter at gitterkolonnerne er blevet omfordelt via tilpasning.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-169">The legacy behavior for default actions in grids results in an unexpected column having the default action link after grid columns have been reordered via personalization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-170">Den nye funktion for standardtastaturhandlinger retter op på dette.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-170">The new sticky default action feature corrects this.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-171">Du kan finde yderligere oplysninger under [Standardtastaturhandlinger i gitre](https://docs.microsoft.com/business-applications-release-notes/October18/dynamics365-finance-operations/sticky-default-action).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-171">For more details, see [Sticky default actions in grids](https://docs.microsoft.com/business-applications-release-notes/October18/dynamics365-finance-operations/sticky-default-action).</span></span> |

### <a name="parameter-to-enable-sales-orders-with-multiple-project-contract-funding-sources"></a><span data-ttu-id="75868-193">Parameter til at aktivere salgsordre for projektkontrakter med flere finansieringskilder</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-193">Parameter to enable sales orders with multiple project contract funding sources</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="75868-194">Understøttelse til at oprette projektbaserede salgsordre i de tilfælde, hvor projektkontrakten har flere finansieringskilder, er gjort mulig ved hjælp af indstillingen **Projektstyringsparametre** og **Tillad salgsordre for projekter med flere finansieringskilder**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-194">Support for creating project-based sales orders where the project contract has multiple funding sources is enabled with the **Project management parameters** setting **Allow sales orders for project with multiple funding sources**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-195">Dette parameter er ikke aktiveret som standard.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-195">By default, this parameter is not enabled.</span></span> 

|   |  |
|------------|--------------------|

### <a name="deprecated-apis-and-future-breaking-changes"></a><span data-ttu-id="75868-282">Forældede API'er og ændringer, der kan give fremtidige beskadigelser</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-282">Deprecated APIs and future breaking changes</span></span>

#### <a name="field-groups-containing-invalid-field-references"></a><span data-ttu-id="75868-283">Feltgrupper, der indeholder ugyldige feltreferencer</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-283">Field groups containing invalid field references</span></span>

|   |  |
|------------|--------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="75868-284">**Årsagen til forældelsen/fjernelsen**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-284">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="75868-285">Det er muligt for definitioner af tabelmetadata at have feltgrupper, der indeholder ugyldige referencer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-285">It is possible for table metadata definitions to have field groups containing invalid field references.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-286">Dette problem kategoriseres i øjeblikket som en *kompileradvarsel* i stedet for en *fejl*, hvilket betyder, at oprettelsen af den installerbare pakke og installationen kan fortsætte, uden at problemet rettes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-286">This issue is currently categorized as a *compiler warning* rather than an *error*, meaning that the deployable package creation and deployment can proceed without fixing the issue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-287">Hvis pakken installeres, kan det medføre kørselsfejl i Økonomirapportering og SQL Server Reporting Services (SSRS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-287">If deployed, this can cause runtime failures in Financial Reporting and SQL Server Reporting Services (SSRS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-288">Sådan løser du problemet:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-288">To fix this issue:</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="75868-289">1. Fjern den ugyldige feltreference fra definitionen af tabelfeltgruppen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-289">1. Remove the invalid field reference from the table field group definition.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="75868-290">2. Kompiler igen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-290">2. Recompile.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="75868-291">3. ## <a name="dynamics-365-for-retail-72"></a><span data-ttu-id="75868-493">Dynamics 365 for Retail 7.2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-493">Dynamics 365 for Retail 7.2</span></span>

### <a name="personalized-product-recommendations"></a><span data-ttu-id="75868-494">Tilpassede produktanbefalinger</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-494">Personalized product recommendations</span></span> 
<span data-ttu-id="75868-495">Fra og med den 15. februar 2018 vil detailhandlere ikke længere kunne vise personlige produktanbefalinger på en POS-enhed.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-495">Starting February 15, 2018, retailers will no longer be able to display personalized product recommendations on a point of sale (POS) device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-496">Du kan finde flere oplysninger under [Tilpassede produktanbefalinger](../../retail/personalized-product-recommendations.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-496">For more information, see [Personalized product recommendations](../../retail/personalized-product-recommendations.md).</span></span>  

|   |  |

### <a name="data-partitions"></a><span data-ttu-id="75868-1069">Datapartitioner</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1069">Data partitions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="75868-1070">Datapartitioner giver en logisk adskillelse af dataene i Microsoft Dynamics AX-databasen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1070">Data partitions provide a logical separation of data in the Microsoft Dynamics AX database.</span></span>

|   |  |
|------------|--------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="75868-1071">**Årsagen til forældelsen/fjernelsen**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1071">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="75868-1072">Datapartitioner blev introduceret i Microsoft Dynamics AX 2012 R2 for at give mulighed for dataisolering.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1072">Data partitions were introduced in Microsoft Dynamics AX 2012 R2 to enable data isolation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-1073">I et almindeligt scenarie har en virksomhed datterselskaber, og data fra ét datterselskab bør ikke være synlige for et andet datterselskab, selvom begge datterselskaber, der administreres af samme it-afdeling.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1073">In a common scenario, a company has subsidiaries, and the data from one subsidiary should not be visible to another subsidiary, even though both subsidiaries are managed by the same IT department.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-1074">Dog var ekstra scripts og indirekte administrationsomkostninger i hele programmet påkrævet for at oprette nye partitioner og udfylde dem med data og til sikkerhedskopiering af data på partitionen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1074">However, extra scripts and management overhead throughout the program were required in order to create new partitions and populate them with data, and to back up partition data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-1075">I skyen, hvor vi har adgang til PaaS-databasetjenester (platform som en tjeneste) (Microsoft Azure, SQL Database), er det langt mere effektivt at bruge en database som isolationscontainer end at udføre isolation i programmet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1075">In the cloud, where we have access to platform as a service (PaaS) database services (Microsoft Azure SQL Database), it's much more efficient to use a database as the isolation container than to do isolation in the program.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-1076">Uanset om datapartitionering er påkrævet for datterselskaber, for flere lejere eller blot af skaleringsårsager, mener vi, at scenarierne kan håndteres bedre gennem flere Finance and Operations-forekomster.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1076">Regardless of whether data partitioning is required for subsidiaries, for multiple tenants, or just for scale, we believe that the scenarios can be handled better through multiple instances of Finance and Operations.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="75868-1077">**Erstattet af en anden funktion?**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1077">**Replaced by another feature?**</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="75868-1078">Kunder, der bruger datapartitioner, skal bruge flere forekomster af Finance and Operations, hvis separation på databaseniveau er af vigtighed.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1078">Customers using data partitions must use multiple instances of Finance and Operations if database level separation is a critical issue.</span></span>    |
| <span data-ttu-id="75868-1079">**Produktområder, der er berørt**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1079">**Product areas affected**</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="75868-1080">Alle moduler</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1080">All modules</span></span>  |

### <a name="dutch-swift-mt940"></a><span data-ttu-id="75868-1129">Nederlandsk SWIFT MT940</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1129">Dutch SWIFT MT940</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="75868-1307">Product Builder blev brugt til at konfigurere varer dynamisk fra en salgsordre, en indkøbsordre, en produktionsordre, et salgstilbud, et projekttilbud eller et varebehov.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1307">Product builder was used to dynamically configure items from a sales order, purchase order, production order, sales quotation, project quotation, or item requirement.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-1308">Baseret på en produktmodel, der havde modelvariabler, kunne brugeren vælge værdier, der opfyldte kundekrav og få en entydig produktvariant, der havde en stykliste og rute.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1308">Based on a product model that had modeling variables, the user could select values to meet the customer requirements and get a unique product variant that had a BOM and route.</span></span>

### <a name="virtual-company-accounts"></a><span data-ttu-id="75868-1404">Virtuelle regnskaber</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1404">Virtual company accounts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="75868-1405">Funktionen til virtuelle regnskaber understøttes ikke længere i Dynamics AX.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1405">The virtual companies feature is no longer supported in Dynamics AX.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-1406">Funktionen til virtuelle regnskaber gør det muligt for brugere at oprette tabeller, der skulle deles med en række regnskaber.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1406">The virtual companies feature let users set up tables that could be shared by a set of companies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-1407">Du kan finde en beskrivelse af funktionen her: [Regnskaber og virtuelle regnskaber](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/aa834382(v=ax.10).aspx).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1407">For a description of the feature, see [Company accounts and Virtual company accounts](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/aa834382(v=ax.10).aspx).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-1408">Funktionen fungerer ved at gruppere tabeller i samlinger, der er tildelt til virtuelle regnskaber, som er grupper af eksisterende "reelle" regnskaber.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1408">The feature works by grouping tables into collections that are assigned to virtual companies, which are groups of existing “real” companies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="75868-1409">Forespørgsler oprettes, så alle regnskaber i det virtuelle regnskab kan få adgang til dataene i tabellerne i de tilknyttede tabelsamlinger.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="75868-1409">Queries are created so that all the companies in the virtual company can access the data in the tables of the associated table collections.</span></span>
